\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a6f42e8dcf4590a6fc74c84a70cd1b1b1}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a6f42e8dcf4590a6fc74c84a70cd1b1b1}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!motor\_set\_zero\_position@{motor\_set\_zero\_position}}
\index{motor\_set\_zero\_position@{motor\_set\_zero\_position}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{motor\_set\_zero\_position()}{motor\_set\_zero\_position()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::motor\+\_\+set\+\_\+zero\+\_\+position (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{const double}]{position }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the position for the motor in its encoder units. 

This will be the future reference point for the motor\textquotesingle{}s \char`\"{}absolute\char`\"{} position.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em position} & The new reference position in its encoder units\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}

 \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ae116783bc7e5a65b336d8ce2972a720f}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ae116783bc7e5a65b336d8ce2972a720f}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!\_\_attribute\_\_@{\_\_attribute\_\_}}
\index{\_\_attribute\_\_@{\_\_attribute\_\_}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_attribute\_\_()}{\_\_attribute\_\_()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__full__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+full\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} \+\_\+\+\_\+attribute\+\_\+\+\_\+ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(deprecated(\char`\"{}Changing these values is not supported by V\+EX and may lead to permanent motor damage.\char`\"{}))}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Takes in floating point values and returns a properly formatted pid struct. 

Gets the velocity P\+ID that was set for the motor.

Gets the position P\+ID that was set for the motor.

Sets one of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__full__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+full\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} for the motor.

Sets one of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} for the motor.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} struct is in 4.\+4 format, i.\+e. 0x20 is 2.\+0, 0x21 is 2.\+0625, etc. This function will convert the floating point values to the nearest 4.\+4 value.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em kf} & The feedforward constant \\
\hline
{\em kp} & The proportional constant \\
\hline
{\em ki} & The integral constant \\
\hline
{\em kd} & The derivative constant\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} struct formatted properly in 4.\+4.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} struct is in 4.\+4 format, i.\+e. 0x20 is 2.\+0, 0x21 is 2.\+0625, etc. This function will convert the floating point values to the nearest 4.\+4 value.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em kf} & The feedforward constant \\
\hline
{\em kp} & The proportional constant \\
\hline
{\em ki} & The integral constant \\
\hline
{\em kd} & The derivative constant \\
\hline
{\em filter} & A constant used for filtering the profile acceleration \\
\hline
{\em limit} & The integral limit \\
\hline
{\em threshold} & The threshold for determining if a position movement has reached its goal. This has no effect for velocity P\+ID calculations. \\
\hline
{\em loopspeed} & The rate at which the P\+ID computation is run in ms\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_3globalScope_4_structmotor__pid__s__t}{motor\+\_\+pid\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} struct formatted properly in 4.\+4.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This intended to just modify the main P\+ID constants.

Only non-\/zero values of the struct will change the existing motor constants.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This feature is in beta, it is advised to use caution when modifying the P\+ID values. The motor could be damaged by particularly large constants.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em pid} & The new motor P\+ID constants\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Only non-\/zero values of the struct will change the existing motor constants.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This feature is in beta, it is advised to use caution when modifying the P\+ID values. The motor could be damaged by particularly large constants.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em pid} & The new motor P\+ID constants\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function will return zero for all of the parameters if the motor\+\_\+set\+\_\+pos\+\_\+pid() or motor\+\_\+set\+\_\+pos\+\_\+pid\+\_\+full() functions have not been used.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor

Additionally, in an error state all values of the returned struct are set to their negative maximum values.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{motor\_get\_encoder\_units()}{motor\_get\_encoder\_units()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily motor\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+units\+\_\+e\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::motor\+\_\+get\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+units (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the encoder units that were set for the motor. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
One of motor\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+units\+\_\+e\+\_\+t according to what is set for the motor or E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+E\+N\+C\+O\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L\+ID if the operation failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a568fdf3db5acd5a58a289222fa13788a}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a568fdf3db5acd5a58a289222fa13788a}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{motor\_is\_reversed()}{motor\_is\_reversed()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::motor\+\_\+is\+\_\+reversed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the operation direction of the motor as set by the user. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the motor has been reversed and 0 if the motor was not reversed, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}
{\bfseries{Example}}

 \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a13462c28c1a64cbcb5da656b60ee3f96}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a13462c28c1a64cbcb5da656b60ee3f96}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!motor\_get\_voltage\_limit@{motor\_get\_voltage\_limit}}
\index{motor\_get\_voltage\_limit@{motor\_get\_voltage\_limit}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{motor\_get\_voltage\_limit()}{motor\_get\_voltage\_limit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::motor\+\_\+get\+\_\+voltage\+\_\+limit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the voltage limit set by the user. 

Default value is 0V, which means that there is no software limitation imposed on the voltage.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The motor\textquotesingle{}s voltage limit in V or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.
\end{DoxyReturn}
{\bfseries{Example}} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{// Prints 0 by default, indicating no limit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\end{DoxyCode}
